# Danny Salman

Technical enablement, DX, and knowledge systems for protocols, platforms, and emerging technologies.

## E8 Root System

The [E8 root system](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/E8_(mathematics)) — 240 vertices in 8-dimensional space, projected to 3D. Each vertex is a root vector; edges connect roots whose inner product equals 1. Rotate, zoom, and pan the model below.

```stl
solid e8lattice
facet normal 0.58 0.58 0.58
 outer loop
  vertex -30.76 0.39 5.10
  vertex -31.21 0.84 5.10
  vertex -31.21 0.39 5.55
 endloop
endfacet
facet normal 0.58 -0.58 0.58
 outer loop
  vertex -30.76 0.39 5.10
  vertex -31.21 0.39 5.55
  vertex -31.21 -0.06 5.10
 endloop
```
